# Surrogate pairs

.		"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
.	u	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
.	v	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"

💩		"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
💩	u	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
💩	v	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"

💩?		"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
💩?	u	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
💩?	v	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"

(💩|💫)+		"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
(💩|💫)+	u	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"
(💩|💫)+	v	"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"

\ud83d\udca9?		"\ud83d💩💫💩\udca9"

# Common character escape sequences

\t\r\n\v\f		"\0\t\r\n\v\f\b"

# RegExp modifiers ((?ims-ims:pattern))

## Basic ignoreCase modifier
(?i:abc)		ABC
(?i:abc)		abc
(?i:abc)		AbC
(?i:abc)	u	ABC
(?i:abc)	v	ABC
(?i:abc)	u	abc
(?i:abc)	v	abc

## Basic multiline modifier
(?m:^a)		"b\na"
(?m:a$)		"a\nb"
(?m:^a$)		"b\na\nb"

## Basic dotAll modifier
(?s:.)		"\n"
(?s:.)		a
(?s:.)		"\r"

## Remove modifiers
(?-i:abc)	i	abc
(?-i:abc)	i	ABC
(?-s:.)	s	a
(?-s:.)	s	"\n"
(?-m:^a)	m	"b\na"
(?-m:^a)	m	a

## Combined add modifiers
(?im:^abc)		"b\nabc"
(?im:^abc)		"b\nABC"
(?is:.abc)		"\nabc"
(?is:.abc)		"\nABC"
(?ims:^.a)		"b\n\na"

## Add + remove modifiers
(?i-m:^abc)	m	abc
(?i-m:^abc)	m	ABC
(?i-m:^abc)	m	"b\nabc"
(?m-i:^abc)	i	"b\nabc"
(?m-i:^abc)	i	"b\nABC"

## Empty remove syntax
(?s-:.)		"\n"
(?s-:.)		a
(?m-:^a)		"b\na"

## Scoping — modifier only applies inside group
a(?i:b)c		aBc
a(?i:b)c		ABc
a(?i:b)c		aBC
a(?i:b)c		abc

## Nested modifier groups
(?s:(?-s:.).)		"a\n"
(?s:(?-s:.).)		"\n\n"
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		aB
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		AB
(?i:(?-i:a)b)		ab

## Quantifier after modifier group
(?i:a)+		aAaA
(?s:.){2}		"a\n"
(?i:a)*		aA

## Alternation inside modifier group
(?i:a|B)		a
(?i:a|B)		b
(?i:a|B)		A
(?i:a|B)		B

## Capturing group inside modifier group
(?i:(a)b)		AB

# With u flag
(?i:abc)	u	AbC
(?i:abc)	v	AbC
(?s:.)	u	"\n"
(?s:.)	v	"\n"
(?m:^a)	u	"b\na"
(?m:^a)	v	"b\na"

## Error cases (these should produce syntax errors)
(?z:a)		a
(?ii:a)		a
(?i-i:a)		a
(?i-s-i:a)		a
(?-:a)		a
(?I:a)		a
(?1:a)		a
(?-ss:a)		a
(?mm:a)		a

## Sequential modifier groups
(?i:a)(?s:.)		"A\n"
(?i:a)b		Ab

## Empty content modifier groups
(?i:)		a
(?s:)		a
(?m:)		a

## Class set disjunction edge cases

\q	v	q
\q{	v	q{	!ignore-error-message
\q{}	v	\q{}

[\q]	v	[q]
[\q{]	v	[q{]
[\q{}]	v	 
[\q{ }]	v	 
[\q{|}]	v	  
[\q{ | }]	v	  
[\q{-}]	v	-
[\q{--}]	v	--
[\q{&}]	v	&
[\q{&&}]	v	&&
[\q{#}]	v	##
[\q{##}]	v	##
[\q{/}]	v	//
[\q{/}]	v	//
[\q{\}]	v	\\
[\q{\}]	v	\\
[\q{\0}]	v	0
[\q{\d}]	v	0
[\q{\p{Sc}}]	v	0
[\q{\q{0}}]	v	0

[^\q{}]	v	abc
[^\q{a}]	v	abc
[^\q{ab|c}]	v	abc
[^\q{a|b|c}]	v	abc

[[^\q{}]]	v	abc
[[^\q{a}]]	v	abc
[[^\q{ab|c}]]	v	abc
[[^\q{a|b|c}]]	v	abc

/[^\q{a}--\q{a}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a}--\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab}--\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab}--\q{a}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab|c}--\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a|b|c}--\q{ab}]/v	v	abc

/[^[\q{a}]--[\q{a}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{a}]--[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab}]--[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab}]--[\q{a}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab|c}]--[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{a|b|c}]--[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a}&&\q{a}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a}&&\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab}&&\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab}&&\q{a}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab|c}&&\q{ab}]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a|b|c}&&\q{ab}]/v	v	abc

/[^[\q{a}]&&[\q{a}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{a}]&&[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab}]&&[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab}]&&[\q{a}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{ab|c}]&&[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc
/[^[\q{a|b|c}]&&[\q{ab}]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a}--[\q{b}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab|c}--[\q{ab}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a|b|c}--[\q{ab}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a}--[\q{b}&&[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab|c}--[\q{ab}&&[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a|b|c}--[\q{ab}&&[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a}&&[\q{b}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{ab|c}&&[\q{ab}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc
/[^\q{a|b|c}&&[\q{ab}--[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a}&&[\q{b}&&[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc

/[^\q{a|b|c}&&[\q{ab}&&[\q{c}]]]/v	v	abc

# Class set success cases

[a\\-b]	v	abc123

[a&&b]	v	abc123
[a--b]	v	abc123
[[a-z]&&[aeiou]]	v	abc123
[[a-z]--[aeiou]]	v	abc123
[[a-f][0-9]]	v	abc123
[[[a-f]--[b]][0-9]]	v	abc123
[\\p{Decimal_Number}&&[0-9]]	v	abc123


[\\q{a}]	v	abc123
[\\q{a|}]	v	abc123
[\\q{|a}]	v	abc123
[\\q{abc|def}]	v	abc123
[\\q{abc|d|ef}]	v	abc123
